       <div id="left-area">
        <article class="entry-content clearfix">
         <h1 class="main-title">
          Premenopausal Symptoms  Examples of Premenopausal Symptoms
         </h1>
         <div class="rating " data-post="9047">
          <div itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
           <span itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
            <span itemprop="name" style="display:none;">
             Lisiana Carter
            </span>
           </span>
           <!-- &lt;span&gt;Author: &lt;/span&gt;-->
           <span itemprop="itemReviewed">
            <span itemprop="name" style="display:none">
             Premenopausal Symptoms  Examples of Premenopausal Symptoms
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="description" style="display:none">
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="adsby-ggl">
          <div class="addtitle">
           Advertisement
          </div>
          <script async="" src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js">
          </script>
          <!-- CHD-Responsive-Heading -->
          <ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-6499174231313712" data-ad-format="auto" data-ad-slot="7933082198" style="display:block">
          </ins>
          <script>
           (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
          </script>
         </div>
         <p>
          When left to nature a woman typically does not start menopause until she is between 45 and 55. However, women who are undergoing certain medical treatments, have certain illnesses, or a history of early menopause may start the menopausal process earlier. Women who start to exhibit signs and symptoms of menopause between 30 and 45 are considered to be in a stage of life known as premenopause. The following are some examples of premenopausal symptoms women who are suffering from early onset menopause may experience.
         </p>

             </a>
             <span>
              <a href="https://www.consumerhealthdigest.com/menopause-supplement-reviews/i-cool-d.html" title="i-cool + D">
               Read Full Review About i-cool + D
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
           </section>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="postwidth">
          <img alt="Premenopausal Symptoms" data-lazy-src="/wp-content/uploads/2012/01/premenopausal-symptoms.jpg" src="https://www.consumerhealthdigest.com/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="Premenopausal Symptoms" src="/wp-content/uploads/2012/01/premenopausal-symptoms.jpg"/>
          </noscript>
         </div>
         <p>
          Changes in menstrual cycles are the most common type of premenopausal symptoms women experience. Menstrual cycle changes can vary from experiencing heavier or lighter periods, having menstrual cycles closer or father apart, or experiencing spotting between periods. The changes in menstrual cycles are a result of the body starting to slowly shut down the ovaries. Ovaries that are shutting down will start to produce lower levels of estrogen. Low levels of estrogen prevent the body from keeping menstrual cycles regular. Some menstrual cycle changes such as extremely heavy bleeding, blood clots and bleeding during sex are not premenopausal symptoms. It is important to seek the help of a healthcare professional or a doctor if you experience these menstrual cycle changes.
         </p>
         <p>
          Low levels of estrogen and fluctuating hormone levels cause women to experience other premenstrual symptoms besides menstrual cycle changes. Other premenopausal symptoms include vaginal dryness, painful intercourse, itching and burning around the vagina, dry skin, weight gain, dry eyes, insomnia, fatigue,
          <a href="/menopause-center/hot-flashes.html">
           hot flashes
          </a>
          and tender breasts. Psychological premenopausal symptoms are also common. Psychological symptoms of early onset menopause include mood swings, mild depression, and anxiety. Some women may also have trouble coping emotionally with the early onset of menopause which can cause extreme depression or anxiety.
         </p>
         <p>
          There is no way to medically reverse the early onset of menopause. However, healthcare providers and doctors can help women treat and manage premenopausal symptoms. The type of treatment recommended to treat premenopausal symptoms will vary depending upon what symptoms a woman experiences, and the severity of those symptoms. Treatment options can include
          <a href="/menopause-center/hormone-replacement-therapy.html">
           hormone replacement therapy
          </a>
          , low-dose birth control pills, herbal supplements designed to naturally raise hormone levels, low-dose antidepressants, and alternative medical procedures such as chiropractic procedures, acupuncture and massage therapy. Women who are having difficulty coping with premature menopause may wish to see a counselor or therapist who can help them deal with the early onset of menopause.
         </p>

  <!--parent script start -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   function DoNav(theUrl)

{

document.location.href = theUrl;

}



function getCookie(c_name)

{

var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");

for (i=0;i&lt;ARRcookies.length;i++)

{

x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));

y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);

x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");

if (x==c_name)

{

return unescape(y);

}

}

}



function setCookie(c_name,value,exdays , setterm )

{

var exdate=new Date();

var time = exdate.getTime();

var path = "/";



if( 'D' === setterm )

{

exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);

}

else if( 'H' === setterm )

{

time += (exdays * 3600) * 1000;

exdate.setTime(time);

}

var c_value=escape(value) + ((exdays==null) ? "" : "; expires="+exdate.toUTCString()+"; path="+path);

document.cookie=c_name + "=" + c_value;



}





function setParentSiteReference()

{

var url=document.location+"";



var urlParts=url.split("/");



url=urlParts[urlParts.length-1];

var source="";

if(urlParts[urlParts.length-1].indexOf("source=")!=-1)

{

source="/"+urlParts[urlParts.length-1].substring(urlParts[urlParts.length-1].indexOf("source=")+7,100);

}

var cookieValue=decodeURIComponent(url.substring(0,url.indexOf(".htm")))+source;



if(url.indexOf(".htm")==-1)

{

cookieValue= decodeURIComponent(url.substring(0,100))+source;

}



var checkcookie = getCookie("parentSiteReference");



if(checkcookie != null &amp;&amp; checkcookie != '')

{ 

    setCookie("parentSiteReference",cookieValue,3,'H');

}

else

{

     setCookie("parentSiteReference",cookieValue,3,'H');

    //  setCookie("parentSiteReference",cookieValue,1,'D'); Day expiring

}



}

setParentSiteReference();
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function CheckData(){
	
	if(document.getElementById('email2').value == "" || document.getElementById('email2').value == "Mail")
	  {
		alert("Please Enter email.");
		return false;
	  }
		strEmail=new String(document.getElementById('email2').value);
	if(strEmail.length&lt;5 || strEmail.indexOf("@")==-1 || strEmail.indexOf(".")==-1)
   	  {
		alert("Please enter a valid Email ID");
		return false;
	  }
	  //  document.form1.submit();
	return true;
}
